You said:
CMO: This is solid infrastructure thinking. A few reactions:

**What's right:**

The core architecture — static hosting, deterministic URLs, Google Apps Script for email delivery — is the correct choice for your scale. Zero SaaS dependency, zero recurring cost, and it deploys through the same CI pipeline as everything else. The separation between "audiobook never forces email / landing page does" is exactly right for platform compliance.

**What needs adjustment:**

**Google Forms is the wrong MVP.** The doc recommends Google Forms as the fastest option, but it breaks your brand experience completely. A listener finishes a beautifully voiced 8-hour deep dive, taps a CTA, and lands on... a generic Google Form. That's a trust fracture. Option B (static HTML form → Apps Script endpoint → Google Sheet → auto-email) should be your V1, not your V2. The implementation cost difference is maybe 2 hours, and you already have a generator that can template HTML pages.

**The email list is more valuable than the doc acknowledges.** This plan treats email collection as a nice-to-have side effect. For a 1,008-book catalog with 60 free titles and companion workbooks on every deep dive, you're looking at potentially thousands of email captures per month at steady-state. That's not a "follow-up sequence" footnote — that's your owned audience channel. When you launch Wave 2 brands, you can notify people who downloaded Wave 1 freebies in related clusters. This should be designed as a first-class data asset from Day 1, which means tagging every capture with book_id, brand_id, teacher_id, and cluster so you can segment later.

**Missing: what happens after email capture.** The doc stops at "optional follow-up sequence." For your model, the follow-up should be automatic and simple — one email 7 days after download that says "here are 3 more titles from [teacher] in [brand]" with direct Google Play links. Not a drip campaign, not a newsletter. One email, one nudge, automated per-book. Your generator can produce these at plan-time alongside the workbook.

**The exercise app gating call is correct.** Don't gate exercise apps. They're in-session tools. Gating them mid-listen would be like putting a paywall inside a meditation. Workbooks and PDFs are the right gating targets — they feel like gifts worth an email address.

**One thing to watch:** Google Apps Script has a daily email send limit of 100 (free Gmail) or 1,500 (Google Workspace). If you're capturing more than that, you'll need to batch sends or use a transactional email service like Postmark ($1.25/1,000 emails). Worth noting in the ops doc so it doesn't surprise you at scale.

Bottom line — build Option B as your V1, tag every capture for segmentation, add one automated follow-up email per freebie, and treat the email list as a revenue asset, not a courtesy feature. The rest is correct and ready to implement.

DELIVERABLE 1 — Google Apps Script (READY TO PASTE)
Purpose
Collect email
Store metadata
Send workbook
Schedule 7-day follow-up
Google Sheet columns (first row)
email | book_id | brand_id | teacher_id | cluster | freebie_type | created_at | followup_sent
Apps Script (Code.gs)
const SHEET_NAME = "captures";
const FOLLOWUP_DELAY_DAYS = 7;

function doPost(e) {
  const data = JSON.parse(e.postData.contents);

  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  sheet.appendRow([
    data.email,
    data.book_id,
    data.brand_id,
    data.teacher_id,
    data.cluster,
    data.freebie_type,
    new Date().toISOString(),
    false
  ]);

  sendImmediateEmail(data);
  scheduleFollowup(data);

  return ContentService
    .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ status: "ok" }))
    .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

function sendImmediateEmail(data) {
  const subject = "Your free companion workbook";
  const body = `
Hi,

Here’s your free companion workbook.

Download:
${data.download_url}

Take care,
${data.teacher_id}
`;

  GmailApp.sendEmail(data.email, subject, body);
}

function scheduleFollowup(data) {
  const triggerTime = new Date();
  triggerTime.setDate(triggerTime.getDate() + FOLLOWUP_DELAY_DAYS);

  ScriptApp.newTrigger("sendFollowup")
    .timeBased()
    .at(triggerTime)
    .create();

  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties()
    .setProperty(`followup_${data.email}_${data.book_id}`, JSON.stringify(data));
}

function sendFollowup() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();

  for (const key in props) {
    if (!key.startsWith("followup_")) continue;

    const data = JSON.parse(props[key]);

    const subject = `More from ${data.teacher_id}`;
    const body = `
Hi,

If you found the workbook helpful, here are three related titles:

• ${data.related_1}
• ${data.related_2}
• ${data.related_3}

Take care,
${data.teacher_id}
`;

    GmailApp.sendEmail(data.email, subject, body);
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty(key);
  }
}

One per brand
Stored at:

  <input type="hidden" name="freebie_type" value="companion_workbook">

  <button type="submit">Get the workbook</button>
</form>

<script>
const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

document.querySelectorAll("input[name]").forEach(el => {
  if (params.has(el.name)) el.value = params.get(el.name);
});

document.getElementById("freebieForm").addEventListener("submit", async (e) => {
  e.preventDefault();
  const data = Object.fromEntries(new FormData(e.target));

  await fetch("https://script.google.com/macros/s/YOUR_SCRIPT_ID/exec", {
    method: "POST",
    body: JSON.stringify(data)
  });

  document.body.innerHTML = "<h3>Check your email ✨</h3>";
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

You said:
CMO: The architecture is correct. One template per brand, parameterized per book, static hosting, single Apps Script backend — that's the right design. A few things to flag:

**The Apps Script has a real bug.** The scheduleFollowup function creates a new time-based trigger for every single email capture. Google Apps Script has a limit of 20 triggers per script. After 20 freebie downloads, your follow-up system silently breaks. The fix is straightforward: instead of per-capture triggers, run a single daily cron trigger that scans the Google Sheet for rows where followup_sent == false and created_at is older than 7 days, then sends and marks them. One trigger, unlimited scale.

**The PropertiesService approach won't scale either.** Script properties have a total storage limit of 500KB. Storing full JSON blobs per capture will hit that ceiling fast. Since you're already writing to a Sheet, just read from the Sheet in your daily cron. The Sheet *is* your database — don't duplicate state in properties.

**The landing page HTML is too bare.** It works mechanically, but a system-ui font on a white page with no brand identity will feel like a phishing page to someone who just finished a beautifully voiced somatic healing session. Each brand template needs at minimum the brand's color palette from your cover art identity spec, the teacher name displayed (not just in a hidden field), and a one-line description pulled from the book's emotional vocabulary. Your generator already has all this data — it just needs to inject it into the template. This doesn't mean 24 bespoke designs. It means one HTML template with CSS variables that get populated per brand at generation time.

**The URL scheme choice matters more than the doc suggests.** Go with the pretty version (/free/{brand_id}/companion/{book_id}/) and generate actual index.html files in those directories. The query-string version (?book_id=...) means your hidden form fields depend on JavaScript parsing URL params. If JS fails to load or a privacy browser strips query strings, your form submits with empty metadata and you get useless captures. Static files with baked-in values are more reliable and cost nothing extra since your generator produces them anyway.

**Missing: unsubscribe handling.** Any automated email system — even a single follow-up — needs a way to opt out. CAN-SPAM requires it, and Google will eventually flag your sending domain if people mark follow-ups as spam because there's no unsubscribe link. Add a simple "Don't want more emails? Reply STOP" line to the follow-up template, and have your daily cron check a "stopped" column before sending.

**The generator extension output is clean.** Landing URL, download URL, and related titles — that's the right data contract. The assembler only sees landing_url, everything else stays downstream. Good separation.

So: fix the trigger architecture (daily cron, not per-capture), drop the PropertiesService hack, brand the templates with CSS variables, use static file paths instead of query strings, add unsubscribe handling, and it's ready to build.

Daily follow-up scanner
function dailyFollowupScan() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActive()
    .getSheetByName("captures");
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const now = new Date();

  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    const [
      email, book_id, brand_id, teacher_id,
      cluster, freebie_type, created_at,
      followup_sent, stopped
    ] = rows[i];

    if (stopped === true) continue;
    if (followup_sent === true) continue;

    const created = new Date(created_at);
    const days = (now - created) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);

    if (days >= 7) {
      sendFollowupEmail(email, book_id, teacher_id);
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 8).setValue(true); // followup_sent
    }
  }
}

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Generate branded landing pages (static HTML) for email-gated freebies.
- One template, parameterized per brand + per book_id
- No querystring dependency: metadata is baked into each index.html
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import argparse
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict

import yaml
from jinja2 import Template

DEFAULT_PALETTE_TOKEN_MAP = {
    # fallback map for palette tokens in brand registry
    "white": "#ffffff",
    "cream": "#f6f1e8",
    "sand": "#eadfcf",
    "soft_blue": "#9bb8d3",
    "sage": "#8aa79b",
    "terracotta": "#c26a4a",
    "navy": "#0f2440",
    "charcoal": "#1f2328",
    "gold": "#c9a227",
    "deep_blue": "#0b2a4a",
    "black": "#0b0b0b",
    "warm_gray": "#b8b0a6",
    "soft_green": "#8fb39a",
    "bright_white": "#ffffff",
    "dark_gray": "#2b2b2b",
    "pastel": "#f2cfe3",
    "bright_accent": "#ff5aa5",
    "teal": "#167c80",
    "forest_green": "#1f5c3a",
    "deep_magenta": "#7b1e5b",
    "burnt_orange": "#c65a1e",
    "raw_canvas": "#efe3cf",
    "chrysalis_gold": "#c9a227",
    "deep_plum": "#3b163f",
    "new_green": "#2f8f4e",
    "accent": "#ffcc00",
}

LANDING_TEMPLATE = Template(r"""<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1" />
  <title>{{ brand_name }} — Free Companion</title>
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="/_assets/base.css" />
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="/_assets/brands/{{ brand_id }}.css" />
</head>
<body>
  <main class="card">
    <header class="header">
      <div class="brand">{{ brand_name }}</div>
      <div class="subtitle">{{ hook_line }}</div>
    </header>

    <section class="content">
      <h1>{{ page_title }}</h1>
      <p class="lede">{{ page_lede }}</p>

      <form id="freebieForm">
        <label>Email address</label>
        <input name="email" type="email" required placeholder="you@email.com" />

        <!-- baked metadata (no querystring dependency) -->
        <input type="hidden" name="book_id" value="{{ book_id }}" />
        <input type="hidden" name="brand_id" value="{{ brand_id }}" />
        <input type="hidden" name="asset_type" value="{{ asset_type }}" />
        <input type="hidden" name="duration_band" value="{{ duration_band }}" />
        <input type="hidden" name="teacher_id" value="{{ teacher_id }}" />
        <input type="hidden" name="topic" value="{{ topic }}" />

        <button type="submit">Send it to my email</button>
      </form>

      <div id="status" class="status" aria-live="polite"></div>

      <p class="fineprint">
        No spam. One follow-up email 7 days later (optional). Reply STOP to opt out.
      </p>
    </section>
  </main>

<script>
(() => {
  const ENDPOINT = "{{ apps_script_webapp_url }}";
  const form = document.getElementById("freebieForm");
  const status = document.getElementById("status");

  form.addEventListener("submit", async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    status.textContent = "Sending…";

    const fd = new FormData(form);
    const payload = {};
    fd.forEach((v,k) => payload[k] = v);

    try {
      const res = await fetch(ENDPOINT, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok || !data.ok) throw new Error(data.error || "Request failed");
      status.textContent = "✅ Check your email — your download link is on the way.";
    } catch (err) {
      status.textContent = "⚠️ Something went wrong. Please try again.";
      console.error(err);
    }
  });
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
""")

def load_yaml(path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))

def safe_mkdir(p: Path) -> None:
    p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def palette_to_css_vars(palette_tokens: list[str], token_map: Dict[str,str]) -> Dict[str,str]:
    # brand registry uses palette tokens like [soft_blue, cream, sage] :contentReference[oaicite:1]{index=1}
    colors = [token_map.get(t, "#888888") for t in palette_tokens]
    primary = colors[0] if colors else "#111111"
    secondary = colors[1] if len(colors) > 1 else "#ffffff"
    accent = colors[2] if len(colors) > 2 else primary
    return {
        "--brand-primary": primary,
        "--brand-surface": secondary,
        "--brand-accent": accent,
    }

def main() -> None:
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--plans", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--brand-registry", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--out", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--apps-script-webapp-url", required=True)
    args = ap.parse_args()

    out_root = Path(args.out)
    safe_mkdir(out_root / "_assets" / "brands")
    safe_mkdir(out_root / "_assets" / "manifest")

    brand_registry = load_yaml(Path(args.brand_registry))
    plans = load_yaml(Path(args.plans))

    # brand registry shape: list of archetypes w/ brand_id and cover_art_identity.color_palette :contentReference[oaicite:2]{index=2}
    # Build brand_id -> identity record (first occurrence wins)
    brand_index: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
    for item in brand_registry.get("archetypes", brand_registry if isinstance(brand_registry, dict) else []):
        bid = item.get("brand_id")
        if bid and bid not in brand_index:
            brand_index[bid] = item

    routes = []
    for bp in plans.get("bookplans", plans if isinstance(plans, dict) else []):
        book_id = bp["book_id"]
        brand_id = bp["brand_id"]
        duration_band = bp.get("duration_band", "mid_form")
        teacher_id = bp.get("teacher_id", "composite")
        topic = bp.get("topic", bp.get("default_topic", "wellness"))

        brand_item = brand_index.get(brand_id, {})
        palette_tokens = (
            brand_item.get("cover_art_identity", {}).get("color_palette")
            or ["charcoal", "white", "accent"]
        )

        # CSS vars per brand
        css_vars = palette_to_css_vars(palette_tokens, DEFAULT_PALETTE_TOKEN_MAP)
        brand_css = "\n".join([f"  {k}: {v};" for k,v in css_vars.items()])
        (out_root / "_assets" / "brands" / f"{brand_id}.css").write_text(
            f":root{{\n{brand_css}\n}}\n", encoding="utf-8"
        )

        brand_name = brand_id.replace("_", " ").title()
        hook_line = f"Free support tools in {brand_name}."
        page_title = "Free Companion Workbook"
        page_lede = "Enter your email and we’ll send the download link instantly."

        # deep_dives = companion landing (CTA #1)
        if duration_band == "deep_dives":
            rel_dir = Path("free") / brand_id / "companion" / book_id
            page = LANDING_TEMPLATE.render(
                brand_id=brand_id,
                brand_name=brand_name,
                hook_line=hook_line,
                page_title=page_title,
                page_lede=page_lede,
                apps_script_webapp_url=args.apps_script_webapp_url,
                book_id=book_id,
                asset_type="companion_workbook",
                duration_band=duration_band,
                teacher_id=teacher_id,
                topic=topic,
            )
            full_dir = out_root / rel_dir
            safe_mkdir(full_dir)
            (full_dir / "index.html").write_text(page, encoding="utf-8")
            routes.append({"book_id": book_id, "brand_id": brand_id, "path": f"/{rel_dir.as_posix()}/"})

        # end-of-book CTA landing (all books): “resources” page (freebie gateway)
        rel_dir2 = Path("free") / brand_id / "resource" / book_id
        page2 = LANDING_TEMPLATE.render(
            brand_id=brand_id,
            brand_name=brand_name,
            hook_line=hook_line,
            page_title="Free Resources",
            page_lede="Enter your email and we’ll send your free resource link.",
            apps_script_webapp_url=args.apps_script_webapp_url,
            book_id=book_id,
            asset_type="end_of_book_resource",
            duration_band=duration_band,
            teacher_id=teacher_id,
            topic=topic,
        )
        full_dir2 = out_root / rel_dir2
        safe_mkdir(full_dir2)
        (full_dir2 / "index.html").write_text(page2, encoding="utf-8")
        routes.append({"book_id": book_id, "brand_id": brand_id, "path": f"/{rel_dir2.as_posix()}/"})

    (out_root / "_assets" / "manifest" / "freebie_routes.json").write_text(
        json.dumps(routes, indent=2), encoding="utf-8"
    )

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
2) Brand CSS variable blocks (from your registry)
Your current brand_archetype_registry_v1_2.yaml provides palette tokens like:
[soft_blue, cream, sage] 
brand_archetype_registry_v1_2
[terracotta, cream, sage] 
brand_archetype_registry_v1_2
So you need:
a token → hex map (fallback)
a predictable variable set used by your landing template
Standard CSS var contract:
:root{
  --brand-primary: #...;
  --brand-surface: #...;
  --brand-accent:  #...;
}
This keeps it “one template, 24 brands”.
(If later you want exact palette control, add an optional cover_art_identity.palette_hex override in brand voice files — but v1 doesn’t require it.)

3) Daily cron + Apps Script (repo artifact)
Create:
ops/google_apps_script/freebie_webapp.gs
What it must do
doPost(e) accepts JSON from landing pages
writes row to Sheet with: email, book_id, brand_id, teacher_id, topic, asset_type, created_at
sends email immediately with a signed download link
daily cron (single trigger) scans for followups due and sends one follow-up
“Reply STOP” support via a stopped column gate (simple + good enough for v1)
Apps Script code (scales; no per-user triggers)
const SHEET_NAME = "captures";
const FOLLOWUP_DAYS = 7;

// Configure these in Script Properties:
// DOWNLOAD_BASE_URL = "https://yourdomain.com/downloads"
// SECRET = "long_random_secret"
// FROM_NAME = "Your Brand System"
// REPLY_TO = "you@yourdomain.com"

function doPost(e) {
  try {
    const body = JSON.parse(e.postData.contents || "{}");
    const email = (body.email || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!email) return jsonOut({ ok:false, error:"Missing email" }, 400);

    const row = {
      created_at: new Date(),
      email: email,
      book_id: body.book_id || "",
      brand_id: body.brand_id || "",
      teacher_id: body.teacher_id || "",
      topic: body.topic || "",
      asset_type: body.asset_type || "",
      followup_sent: false,
      stopped: false
    };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
    const sheet = getOrCreateSheet_(ss);

    // Upsert headers if empty
    ensureHeaders_(sheet, Object.keys(row));

    // Append row
    sheet.appendRow(Object.values(row));

    // Send immediate email with signed link
    const link = buildSignedLink_(row);
    sendImmediate_(row, link);

    return jsonOut({ ok:true });
  } catch (err) {
    return jsonOut({ ok:false, error:String(err) }, 500);
  }
}

function dailyFollowupCron() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const sheet = getOrCreateSheet_(ss);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return;

  const headers = data[0];
  const idx = indexMap_(headers);

  const now = new Date();
  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const stopped = !!row[idx.stopped];
    const followupSent = !!row[idx.followup_sent];
    const createdAt = row[idx.created_at];

    if (stopped || followupSent || !(createdAt instanceof Date)) continue;

    const ageDays = (now - createdAt) / (1000*60*60*24);
    if (ageDays < FOLLOWUP_DAYS) continue;

    const payload = {
      created_at: createdAt,
      email: row[idx.email],
      book_id: row[idx.book_id],
      brand_id: row[idx.brand_id],
      teacher_id: row[idx.teacher_id],
      topic: row[idx.topic],
      asset_type: row[idx.asset_type]
    };

    const link = buildSignedLink_(payload);
    sendFollowup_(payload, link);

    // mark followup sent
    sheet.getRange(r+1, idx.followup_sent+1).setValue(true);
  }
}

function buildSignedLink_(payload) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const base = props.getProperty("DOWNLOAD_BASE_URL"); // e.g. https://yourdomain.com/downloads
  const secret = props.getProperty("SECRET");

  // expire in 24h
  const exp = Math.floor(Date.now()/1000) + 24*60*60;
  const path = resolveAssetPath_(payload); // e.g. /companions/{book_id}.pdf

  const msg = `${payload.email}|${path}|${exp}`;
  const sig = Utilities.base64EncodeWebSafe(
    Utilities.computeHmacSha256Signature(msg, secret)
  );

  // This link points to a tiny “redirect” endpoint you can host as another Apps Script,
  // OR you can directly email the static file if you’re comfortable with it.
  // Recommended: link to /dl?path=...&exp=...&sig=...
  return `${base}/dl?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}&exp=${exp}&sig=${sig}&email=${encodeURIComponent(payload.email)}`;
}

function resolveAssetPath_(p) {
  if (p.asset_type === "companion_workbook") return `/companions/${p.book_id}.pdf`;
  return `/freebies/${p.book_id}.pdf`;
}

function sendImmediate_(p, link) {
  GmailApp.sendEmail(
    p.email,
    "Your free download link",
    `Here’s your link:\n\n${link}\n\nIf you don’t want follow-ups, reply STOP.`,
    { name: PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("FROM_NAME") || "Phoenix Freebies" }
  );
}

function sendFollowup_(p, link) {
  GmailApp.sendEmail(
    p.email,
    "More resources (optional)",
    `Quick follow-up:\n\nHere’s that link again:\n${link}\n\nIf you don’t want future emails, reply STOP.`,
    { name: PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("FROM_NAME") || "Phoenix Freebies" }
  );
}

function jsonOut(obj, code) {
  return ContentService
    .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(obj))
    .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

// Helpers
function getOrCreateSheet_(ss) {
  let sh = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sh) sh = ss.insertSheet(SHEET_NAME);
  return sh;
}
function ensureHeaders_(sheet, headers) {
  const range = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,Math.max(headers.length, sheet.getLastColumn() || 1));
  const row = range.getValues()[0];
  if (row.join("").trim() !== "") return;
  sheet.getRange(1,1,1,headers.length).setValues([headers]);
}
function indexMap_(headers) {
  const m = {};
  headers.forEach((h,i)=> m[String(h).trim()] = i);
  return m;
}
Important: Apps Script sending limits exist (Gmail free ~100/day; Workspace higher). Your earlier note is correct — if you outgrow it, swap the sending function to a transactional provider. But this is perfect for v1.
Where the assembler should point CTAs (your placement rules)
Exercise CTA: link straight to /apps/{app_slug}/index.html (no email gate)
Deep dives CTA #1 (companion workbook): link to /free/{brand_id}/companion/{book_id}/
End-of-book CTA: link to /free/{brand_id}/resource/{book_id}/
This matches your “no spam flags” intent because:
CTAs are stable and deterministic
Landing pages are branded and consistent
Only one follow-up email (optional)
No mid-chapter marketing inserts

brand_archetype_registry_v1_2
 and upgrade later.
